showing open-trade cards, no tabs, no Strategy Dashboard structure, never had a Why It
Skips pane to extend. `git log` confirms: monitor.html has exactly 2 commits total
(initial commit + one "what you changed"), last touched 2026-07-03; index.html has been
under continuous, heavy active development through today (2026-07-06). Per the safety
rule ("if an anchor is missing, STOP and report — do not improvise a similar-looking
location"), this was surfaced to Kev directly before any edit; Kev confirmed: build in
index.html, the phase's file-mapping was the mistake, not the phase's intent.

ALSO FOUND AND FIXED, at Kev's own explicit follow-up request (not part of 7B-2's
original scope, but a direct same-conversation ask, so treated as authorized and done
here rather than deferred): `push_dashboard.py`'s `LOCAL_FILE` constant pointed at
`webapp\monitor.html` — since that script pushes straight to the live chev-monitor
GitHub Pages site, the next time Kev ran it he would have overwritten the live phone
site with a stale, unrelated file instead of the actual current dashboard. Repointed
`LOCAL_FILE` to `webapp\index.html` (one line; `GITHUB_TOKEN` in that file was never
printed, moved, or otherwise touched). *** CAVEAT Kev should weigh before running
push_dashboard.py: index.html is the full 463KB desktop trading terminal (charting
libraries, full watchlist, everything) — it has never been checked as a phone/PWA
experience. Deploying it now means the phone site becomes the entire desktop app, not
a lightweight monitor. monitor.html itself was NOT deleted, only stopped being the
deploy target — trivially revertible if the full desktop app isn't what's wanted on
the phone specifically. ***

THE CHANGE — webapp/index.html only (dexter.py, risk_gauntlet.py, labeller.py,
honest_sim.py, "Chev Prompt" all untouched this phase):
  - New CSS block (added right after the existing `.stratEmptyState` rule):
    `.stratShadowSection` (dashed violet border, `rgba(147,112,219,...)` — a hue used
    nowhere else on the page, so shadow numbers can never be visually mistaken for real
    green/red/gold performance data), `.stratShadowCaveat` (italic, muted), `.stratShadow
    Coverage`, and `.stratBarSplit` + `.right`/`.wrong`/`.pending` (the three-color
    verdict-split fill reused inside the upgraded reason bars — right=`var(--green)`,
    wrong=`var(--red)`, pending=`var(--txt3)`, matching the page's existing palette).
  - New markup inside the `diagnostics` pane (ANCHOR: `<!-- ===== WHY IT SKIPS
    (diagnostics) ===== -->`), directly below the existing `#stratReasonBars` div: a
    `#stratShadowSection` box containing the "🕯️ Shadow Outcomes — hypothetical, costs
    modelled" section label, the verbatim caveat line the quarantine rules require, a
    2-card headline row (🟢 Bullets Dodged / 🔴 Money Left on Table, reusing the existing
    `.stratScoreCard`/`.v.good`/`.v.bad` classes), a coverage line ("N of M resolved"),
    and a `#stratShadowGateGrid` (reusing the existing `.stratGradeGrid`/`.stratGradeCard`
    classes) for the downstream-gate-kill scoreboard.
  - New JS, added directly after `loadFunnel()`, before `loadPerformance()`:
      • `loadShadow()` — fetches `/api/strategy/counterfactual` via the page's own
        `_apiFetch`, fills the headline pair + coverage line, and renders one card per
        `GATE-*` bucket (every downstream kill category the backend provides — COST_GATE,
        PRICE_DRIFT, CONCURRENCY, HEAT_CAP, DATA_QUALITY, NET_RR, CORR_CAP, LIQUIDATION,
        HALLUCINATED_LEVELS, SCORE_GATE, STRUCT_GATE, MTF_TAX, GEOMETRY, OTHER — shown
        individually rather than collapsed into a generic bucket, since the backend
        already provides this granularity), ordered by `|total_r|` descending (currently
        a no-op tiebreak since every gate-kill bucket's `total_r` is 0 by design — no
        Examiner shadow record exists for these, see PHASE 7/7B-1 — but implemented
        correctly for whenever that data shape might change). Every card explicitly
        states "n/a (no Examiner record)" rather than a fake 0% when `shadow_wr` is null
        — matches the .txt report's own honesty convention, not a bug. On fetch failure:
        catches its own error, sets `_shadowBucketsCache = null`, writes "shadow data
        unavailable" into the coverage line, resets the headline numbers to "—", clears
        the gate grid — never throws past its own try/catch, never touches the rest of
        the pane.
      • `applyShadowSplitsToReasonBars()` — upgrades the reason bars `loadFunnel()`
        already rendered, injecting a green/red/grey verdict-split fill INSIDE each bar's
        existing width (the bar's outer length, driven by the raw funnel count, is
        completely unchanged). Matches funnel reason keys to counterfactual bucket keys
        via `SHADOW_DECISION_TO_GATE_KEY` (1:1 renames — `MTF_TAX_REJECT`→`GATE-MTF_TAX`,
        `STRUCT_REJECT`→`GATE-STRUCT_GATE`, `GATE_REJECT`→`GATE-SCORE_GATE`,
        `GEOMETRY_REJECT`→`GATE-GEOMETRY`), `SHADOW_SKIP_KEYS` (the funnel's single "SKIP"
        bar sums the three `SKIP - *` buckets' verdict_split), `SHADOW_BARE_REJECT_KEYS`
        (the funnel's single "REJECT" bar sums every `GATE-*` bucket NOT already covered
        by the direct-rename map), and a direct key match for every raw NOT_ESCALATED
        pre-gate reason (`cooldown`, `choppy_regime`, `below_trade_threshold`, etc. — 1:1,
        no aggregation needed, since the funnel already reports these at the same
        granularity the counterfactual endpoint does). A reason with no matching bucket
        is left completely untouched, exactly as `loadFunnel()` rendered it — per the
        phase's own instruction.
      • `loadAll()` updated to run `loadShadow()` inside the SAME `Promise.all(...)` as
        every other pane load, then call `applyShadowSplitsToReasonBars()` only AFTER
        that Promise.all resolves — deliberately avoiding a race where the bar-splitter
        might run before `loadShadow()` has populated its cache, regardless of which of
        the two fetches happens to finish first. Refresh cadence unchanged: `openStrategy()`
        calls `loadAll()` once on open, then every 25s while the overlay stays open
        (`setInterval(loadAll, 25000)`) — the new fetch rides the exact same cycle as
        `loadFunnel`/`loadPerformance`/etc., matching the existing pattern exactly. The
        counterfactual endpoint's own 300s server-side cache (PHASE 7B-1) means most of
        these 25s polls just hit cache, same as it would for any other pane.
  - Did NOT touch: `loadFunnel()`'s own source (the bar-split upgrade is a separate,
    additive DOM pass, not an edit to its rendering logic), `loadPerformance()`,
    `_tagStatsCache`, the exploration toggle, Firebase config reads, the watchlist sync,
    price feeds, or the trade monitor — all confirmed untouched by inspection.

chars, extracted and checked standalone) — clean, no syntax errors. `<div>` open/close
tag count across the whole file — 510/510, balanced. `python -m py_compile

## SHADOW TAG + COMBO LEADERBOARDS (PHASE 7B-3, 2026-07-06, DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: skips are ~95% of Dexter's escalations — a 15-20x multiplier of labeled
evidence over real trades on which tags/combos precede winning moves, exactly what the
real Combo leaderboard has been starving for (see RISK GAUNTLET / STRATEGY DASHBOARD
sections — almost every real combo sits at n=1-2). But skipped setups are NOT a random
sample — Chev skipped them for reasons — so this is framed throughout as leads for
review, never as a verdict Chev's judgment was wrong.

DISCOVERY: `shadow_tags`/`shadow_combos` already existed on `/api/strategy/counterfactual`
as of PHASE 7B-1 (each entry `{tag|combo, n, resolved, shadow_wr, total_r}`) — no backend
follow-up was needed, confirmed before writing any frontend code. Read the real
leaderboards' render code (inside `loadPerformance()`, dexter's `/api/strategy/
performance` response): tag leaderboard → `#stratTagBars`, filters `s.n >= 3`, sorted by
win_rate descending; combo leaderboard → `#stratComboBars`, `MIN_COMBO_N = 5`, sorted by
raw `n` descending, sliced to 15, greyed via `opacity:0.4` + grey bar + a trailing "⚠"
when untrusted. Both reuse a page-global `winRateColor(pct)` function (0%→red, 50%→gold,
100%→green) and the same `.stratBarRow`/`.stratBarLabel`/`.stratBarTrack`/`.stratBarFill`/
`.stratBarVal` classes the funnel reason bars use.

THE CHANGE — webapp/index.html only:
  - New markup inside `#stratShadowSection` (PHASE 7B-2's box), directly below the gate
    scoreboard grid: "🏷️ Shadow Tag Leaderboard — skipped/killed setups only" + the
    verbatim caveat sentence ("Evidence Chev may be under-trusting these — leads for
    review, not verdicts.", plus the ~95%/15-20x framing from the phase's WHY) +
    `#stratShadowTagBars`, then "🧬 Shadow Combo Leaderboard — skipped/killed setups
    only, greyed out below the shadow trust minimum" + `#stratShadowComboBars`.
  - New CSS: `#stratShadowTagBars .stratBarVal, #stratShadowComboBars .stratBarVal {
    width: 168px; }` — SCOPED to only these two new containers (the real leaderboards'
    shared `.stratBarVal { width: 64px }` rule is completely untouched) because the
    shadow row text is longer ("shadow WR 62% · shadow R +1.23R (n=45)") than the real
    rows' ("62% (n=45)") — every stat label says "shadow," per the quarantine rule, with
    no exceptions, so the value column needed more room, given only to the shadow boards.
  - New JS: `SHADOW_MIN_TAG_N = 10`, `SHADOW_MIN_COMBO_N = 5` (deliberately separate
    constants from the real leaderboards' n>=3 / MIN_COMBO_N=5 — shadow samples are a
    much larger pool, so a higher tag minimum is warranted). `renderShadowLeaderboard
    (elId, entries, kind, minN)` — one shared function for both boards: sorts by
    `total_r` descending (per spec — a DIFFERENT sort than either real leaderboard, which
    sort by win_rate or raw n), slices to 15 for combos / 40 for tags (tags are a small,
    bounded ~30-token vocabulary so effectively unslicing them; combos can run into the
    hundreds, same cap as the real combo leaderboard), greys rows below `resolved < minN`
    (opacity 0.4, grey bar/track, trailing "⚠") — thresholded on `resolved`, never on the
    raw `n` field (which would count still-open records that have no outcome yet). Called
    from inside `loadShadow()` (PHASE 7B-2), reusing the SAME already-fetched
    `/api/strategy/counterfactual` response — no new HTTP request. Reset to empty on
    fetch failure, alongside the rest of `loadShadow()`'s existing failure handling.
  - Did NOT touch: `loadPerformance()`, `d.tag_stats`/`d.combo_stats`, `_tagStatsCache`,
    `#stratTagBars`/`#stratComboBars`, or any other pane's logic — confirmed by direct
    diff: the tag/combo rendering block inside `loadPerformance()` was re-read after this
    phase's edits and is byte-identical to the pre-edit discovery read.

VERIFICATION DONE: `node --check` on the page's full inline `<script>` block — clean.
`<div>` open/close tag count across the whole file — 521/521, balanced (up from 510/510
in PHASE 7B-2, consistent with the new markup added). Real Tag/Combo leaderboard code
diffed line-for-line against the PHASE 7B-2-era read — identical, confirming the
Performance pane is untouched.

## 4-HOUR X-AXIS FOR THE TIME CHARTS (PHASE 25, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: daily buckets hide same-day movement — a threshold change and its effect
on flow, or a run of trades within one day, all collapsed into a single point. Finer
granularity makes cause-and-effect visible within a day, not just across days.

SCHEMA CHANGES (for anything else that reads these endpoints):
- `/api/strategy/timeseries`: new `?bucket_hours=4|24` param (default 4). `rr_pressure`/
  `flow`/`stop_reality` rows now have `t` (epoch int, bucket start) + `label` (human
  string) instead of `date`. `threshold`/`annotations` gained a `t` epoch field alongside
  their existing `ts` string (unchanged, still event-precise, never bucket-aligned).
  Response gained top-level `bucket_hours`. Cache is now keyed on `days` AND
  `bucket_hours` together.
- `/api/strategy/performance`'s `equity_curve`: points are now `{t, cum_pnl}` (epoch +
  running balance per 4h boundary) instead of `{ts, cum_pnl}` (one point per trade).
- `/api/strategy/heatmap`: `grid` is `[7][6]` instead of `[7][24]`; response gained
  `block_hours: 4`.

WHY THE EQUITY CURVE'S FLAT SEGMENTS NEEDED NO NEW RENDERING TRICK: a bucket with no new
close simply repeats the previous bucket's balance as real emitted data — LightweightCharts
draws a flat line between two identical values naturally. No `LineType.WithSteps` needed
(that's still used elsewhere, e.g. the enforced-R:R-floor line, where the semantics are
genuinely "this value held until it changed," a different case).

DELIBERATE SCOPE LIMIT: relying on LightweightCharts' own adaptive tick formatter for the
System Over Time charts (it already switches between date-only and date+time labels
depending on zoom level) rather than writing a custom `tickMarkFormatter`. If Kev's
verification finds the default labeling unclear at some zoom level, that's a small,
well-scoped follow-up — not re-opening this phase.

VERIFICATION: extract-and-exec — 20 backend assertions (bucket_hours default/24/invalid-
fallback, 4h/24h boundary alignment, equity_curve's flat-carry-forward proven with a
2-trades-20h-apart fixture, heatmap's hour→block grouping) plus the exact spot-check Kev's
own STEP 4 asks for: a 9-decision fixture scattered across one calendar day produces
IDENTICAL totals whether summed across six 4h buckets or read from one 24h bucket (9 == 9).
Frontend: `_tsMarkersFor()`'s new floor-to-bucket-boundary matching extracted and
unit-tested in isolation — 4/4 assertions. `python -m py_compile dexter.py` clean.
`node -e` syntax check clean on both `<script>` blocks. `<div>` balance 580/580 (no new
markup — only render logic and one CSS grid rule changed).

KEV VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (verbatim, per STEP 4 — not yet run by Claude, needs a live
restart + browser):
1. Bars/lines on Threshold vs Flow, R:R Pressure, Stop-Distance Reality, and the Equity
   Curve are visibly finer-grained (multiple points per day, not one).
2. Spot-check two real days: sum the six 4h values against what the old daily total would
   have been (or compare `?bucket_hours=24` against `?bucket_hours=4` summed) — must match.
3. Setup Volume heatmap shows 6 columns labeled 00–04 through 20–24; day rows unchanged.
4. Annotation markers (restarts/setting changes) still appear on the right bucket.
5. Console clean; deploy via `push_dashboard.py`, re-check on phone.

## PLAIN-ENGLISH WORDING PASS (PHASE 24, 2026-07-07, DEPLOY REQUIRED, NO RESTART)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: the board should read like English to a stranger, not a code-word
scoreboard. This phase touches nothing about how numbers are computed — copy and layout
only, on the shadow leaderboard rows and four section captions Kev flagged as confusing.

(a) SHADOW LEADERBOARD ROWS — before/after:
  Before: "shadow WR 71% · shadow R +8.28R (n=73)"
  After:  "If taken: won 71% · would've made +8.28R · from 73 setups"
Same source data (`s.shadow_wr`/`s.total_r`/`s.resolved`), same trust-dimming (`opacity`
when `resolved < minN`), same "⚠" marker on untrusted rows — wording and layout only.
Applies to BOTH Shadow Tag and Shadow Combo leaderboards (one shared render function).
Layout: the value phrase now drops to its own line under the label+bar
(`#stratShadowTagBars`/`#stratShadowComboBars .stratBarRow { flex-wrap: wrap }`, the value
cell `width:100%`), and its own three fragments wrap independently within that line if
still too narrow — no `@media` query, pure flexbox reflow, matching this page's existing
convention. Real Tag/Combo Leaderboards (`#stratTagBars`/`#stratComboBars`) are a
completely separate render path (`loadPerformance()`) — untouched.

(b) FOUR CAPTIONS — before/after (caption text; Learn-tab entry mirrors each one, see
`SECTION_TOOLTIPS` in webapp/index.html for the full mirrored text):
  Weekly Regret Trend:
    Before: "— forfeited shadow R per week, full history (not baseline-scoped)"
    After:  "Missed profits by week — what the trades we skipped would have earned.
             Falling is good."
  Shadow Outcomes caveat:
    Before: "Shadow numbers assume perfect fills, no management, no slot limits.
             Evidence for hand-tuning — never merged into real stats."
    After:  "These are "what-if" numbers from trades we did NOT take. They assume
             everything went perfectly — treat them as clues for tuning, never as
             results."
  Equity Curve (had NO caption before — added):
    After:  "Your paper account balance over time — every closed trade moves this line."
  Setup Volume (old detail was baked into the bold label, not a separate caption — moved
  out and replaced):
    Before (part of the bold title): "— Day × Hour (UTC, last 14 days)"
    After (own caption, title simplified to "🗺️ Setup Volume"):
            "When opportunities show up — which days and hours (UTC) the scanner finds
             the most setups."

UNPLANNED FIX FOUND DURING VERIFICATION: `.stratSectionLabel` (shared by all 16 section
headers, not just these four) had no `flex-wrap` — defaulted to `nowrap`, meaning the new,
longer captions (up to ~90 characters) risked overflowing or being squeezed at 380px
instead of wrapping onto their own line, exactly the failure mode this phase's STEP 2 asks
to verify against. Added `flex-wrap: wrap` + a 2-value gap to `.stratSectionLabel` itself —
small, universal, and backward-compatible (only visibly changes anything once content
doesn't fit on one line), so it also protects the 14 sections this phase didn't touch.

VERIFICATION: `node -e` syntax check on both inline `<script>` blocks — clean. `<div>`
balance 580/580 (unchanged — only `<span>` fragments and CSS added). `SECTION_TOOLTIPS`/
`SECTION_ORDER`/markup `data-learn` cross-check still exactly 16/16/16 (values changed,
keys untouched). No Python touched this phase.

## DATA FIXES: EMPTY SCOREBOARD + GATE SCOREBOARD N/A PILLS (PHASE 23, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: two data bugs Kev hit in practice — the Indicator Scoreboard (PHASE 18)
showing zero rows, and every Gate Scoreboard pill reading "n/a ... (no Examiner record)"
regardless of how many decisions fed it. See the top banner for the full diagnosis; this
section is the reference copy of the fix mechanics + the verification checklist.

DIAGNOSIS METHOD, worth remembering for future "why is this empty" bugs: don't trust a
hypothesis (even a well-reasoned one written into the phase spec) without checking it
against REAL data. Bug (a)'s actual cause (shared try/catch, not a join problem) was found
by running the real routes against production chev_journal.json directly. Bug (b)'s
hypothesis was checked by searching the REAL labels_open/closed.jsonl for matches at
multiple time tolerances — and refuted, cleanly, before any code was touched.

BUG (a) FIX — `loadScoreboard()` (webapp/index.html): `Promise.allSettled([...])` instead
of `Promise.all([...])`, each of the 4 sources (tag registry, `/api/strategy/performance`,
`/api/strategy/counterfactual`, `/api/strategy/tag_trends`) handled independently. A
failing Real WR/Shadow WR/Trend source degrades that ONE column to "—" (with an
explanatory `title`) for every row; only a failed registry fetch — the one source every
column actually needs SOMETHING from (Points, the Indicator name) — produces a real empty
state with an explicit message.

BUG (b) FIX:
1. `dexter.py` — one new `labeller.record_setup(result, asset_type, "POST", ...)` call,
   placed immediately after `_trade_originally_parsed = bool(parsed and parsed.get(
   "trade"))` — i.e. the instant Chev's reply first parses as a valid trade, before the
   hallucination guard, score gate, struct gate, MTF tax, geometry review, or risk
   gauntlet ever run. This is a SANCTIONED, Kev-approved exception to the do-not-touch
   list covering labeller call sites — scoped to exactly this one new call, nothing else
   in labeller.py or its other call sites touched. Literal string "POST" is required (not
   a new decision value) because `record_setup()`'s `is_post` check
   (`chev_decision == "POST" and bool(meta.get("direction"))`) is what makes it use
   Chev's own entry/direction instead of the generic confluence-zone proxy every
   NOT_ESCALATED/SKIP record uses — confirmed by reading labeller.py's docstring and
   source (read-only, unedited). The existing symbol+tf+entry_ref dedup (0.5×ATR window,
   already in `record_setup()`) means a trade that goes on to lock in for real collapses
   this into a no-op — no double-counting.
2. `counterfactual_report.py`'s `build_counterfactual()` — the shared bucketing function,
   per the phase's own instruction that this is the ONLY place the fix belongs. The
   downstream gate-kill block (previously: hardcoded `resolved=0, shadow_wr=None` for
   every gate-kill, unconditionally) now looks up the closest "POST" label by
   symbol+tf+timestamp proximity (`GATE_KILL_MATCH_WINDOW_SECS = 900`, 15 minutes —
   comfortably covers Chev's up-to-6-minute deliberation plus retries), matching
   deliberately on proximity ONLY, never on `chev_decision` (requiring the label's
   decision to equal the gate-kill's own decision was the actual historical bug — a
   gate-killed attempt legitimately produces a "POST"-decision label, since the kill
   happens downstream of Chev's own decision, not because of it). A match against a
   resolved (closed-file) label flows through the exact same `bucket_stats()`/
   `_add_bucket()` real-stats machinery every other bucket on the page already uses — no
   new stats math invented. A match against a still-open label, or no match at all
   (every historical gate-kill from before this fix went live), still counts as
   "pending" — the same honest treatment this bucket has always given absent data.
   `_add_bucket()` gained one small, backward-compatible addition: an optional
   `key_override` parameter, so a bucket's public key (`"GATE-COST_GATE"`) can differ from
   the bare code (`"COST_GATE"`) passed to `_bucket_label()` for the friendly text — every
   existing caller omits it and behaves byte-identical to before.

VERIFICATION:
- `counterfactual_report.py --selftest`: new fixture reproducing exactly the case asked
  for (a REJECT decision with symbol="HHH"/tf="1h", a matching "POST" label at the same
  symbol+tf, 120s apart, resolved as a win) — proves the join resolves real numbers:
  `GATE-COST_GATE` now shows n=2 (1 old unmatched + 1 new matched), resolved=1,
  shadow_wr=100%, avg_r/total_r=+0.80, verdict_split right=0/wrong=1/pending=1. A sibling
  bucket with genuinely no matching label anywhere (`GATE-MTF_TAX`) still correctly shows
  resolved=0/shadow_wr=None — proving the fix is additive, not a blanket "always resolve"
  hack. Every existing assertion whose expected total shifted because of the new fixture
  data was recalculated and updated (`coverage.total` 7→11, `coverage.resolved` 6→7,
  `headline.forfeited_r` 2.00→2.80) — **51/51 self-test cases passing** (up from 45).
- `python -m py_compile dexter.py counterfactual_report.py risk_gauntlet.py` — clean.
- Frontend: a standalone Node.js simulation of `loadScoreboard()`'s new logic, stubbing
  `_apiFetch`/`_loadTagRegistry`/`document` — **10/10 assertions**, including reproducing
  the exact historical bug (tag_trends rejecting) and confirming all registry rows still
  render with just that one column degraded, plus confirming the registry-failure case
  correctly shows a real empty-state message rather than a silent blank table.
- `node -e` syntax check on both inline `<script>` blocks — clean. `<div>` balance —
  580/580 (unchanged; this phase only edited existing JS logic, no new markup).

## FRIENDLY NAMES FOR DECISION + REASON CODES (PHASE 22, 2026-07-07, DEPLOY REQUIRED, NO RESTART)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: same philosophy as PHASE 16's tag registry, applied to the OTHER
vocabulary on the board — not "which indicator fired" but "why did this die." Codes like
GATE_REJECT and CONCURRENCY read as code; the registry makes them read as English.

FULL REGISTRY TABLE (code → friendly text, 36 entries):

Decision types:
  GATE_REJECT       Failed pre-checks (Dexter)
  STRUCT_REJECT     No usable structure nearby
  MTF_TAX_REJECT    Against the higher-timeframe trend
  GEOMETRY_REJECT   Chev's numbers didn't hold up (Geometry)
  REJECT            Approved by Chev, killed downstream
  SKIP              Chev passed on it
  FORMAT_ERROR      Chev's reply wasn't in the right format
  POST              Chev posted a trade

Pre-escalation NOT_ESCALATED reasons:
  tf_below_escalation_floor  Timeframe too small (uneconomic)
  below_trade_threshold      Confluence score too low
  below_threshold            Below the cheap first-pass score filter
  struct_pregate             No structural anchor nearby
  too_far_from_level         Price hasn't reached the zone yet
  conflicting_signals        Bullish and bearish signals contradicted
  circuit_breaker            Daily loss limit hit — paused for the day
  cooldown                   Same setup re-fired too soon (cooldown)
  event_block                Paused around a high-impact news release
  choppy_regime              Market too choppy for a directional edge

Gate-kill codes (from counterfactual_report.py's real classifier):
  DATA_QUALITY   Numbers failed sanity check   [corrected from the brief's "ATR_SANITY" — no such code exists]
  COST_GATE      Fees too big for the stop (Cost Gate)
  HEAT_CAP       Total risk cap reached
  CONCURRENCY    Trade slots full
  PRICE_DRIFT    Price moved while Chev decided
  NET_RR         Reward too small after costs (Net R:R)
  CORR_CAP       Too many correlated positions open
  LIQUIDATION    Stop too tight for the leverage used
  HALLUCINATED_LEVELS  Chev's numbers weren't from this chart
  OTHER          Rejected for another reason
  SCORE_GATE     Failed pre-checks (Dexter)
  STRUCT_GATE    No usable structure nearby
  MTF_TAX        Against the higher-timeframe trend
  GEOMETRY       Chev's numbers didn't hold up (Geometry)

Closed-trade close_type (main terminal, outside the Strategy panel):
  TIME_EXIT  Closed by time-stop
  SL_HIT     Stop loss hit
  TP_HIT     Target hit
  SIP_HIT    Stopped in profit (SIP)

WHERE APPLIED (and one deliberate inversion): `#stratReasonBars`, `#stratShadowGateGrid`
show the friendly text visibly with the raw code moved to `title`. Feed cards'
`.stratDecPill` do the OPPOSITE on purpose — it's a small uppercase badge and several
registry entries are full sentences that would break it, so the raw code stays visible
(its original job: a quick-scan color badge) and the friendly text is the `title` instead.
`close_type` in the main terminal log gets the friendly text as an added `title` on its
existing terse TP/SL/SIP label. Raw Log tab: unchanged data, new caption stating the codes
stay verbatim there on purpose. The assembly-line explorer named in the brief doesn't
exist yet (confirmed via grep — never built); `friendlyReason()` will be ready for it.

VERIFICATION: extracted `REASON_REGISTRY`/`friendlyReason()` standalone — 6/6 assertions
(known codes across all four categories resolve correctly, including the DATA_QUALITY
correction; an unrecognized code falls through to the same prettifier PHASE 16's
`friendlyTag()` uses; null/undefined never throws). Registry size confirmed at exactly 36,
matching the full discovered inventory. `node -e` syntax check clean on both script
blocks. `<div>` balance 580/580.

## LEARN TAB (PHASE 21, 2026-07-07, DEPLOY REQUIRED, NO RESTART)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: two problems in one — the Glossary (Concept + Tag) couldn't scroll past
its first screen on either desktop or phone, and Learning Mode's tap-tooltip-per-icon
design meant reading fifteen different one-liners one at a time instead of having
everything in one referenceable place. A Learn tab fixes both: real scrolling (it's just
another pane now) and a deep-link instead of a popup.

ROOT CAUSE (confirmed, not guessed): `#stratGlossary` was a plain flex sibling of
`#stratBody`, not one of its `.stratPane` children. `#strategyPanel{height:92vh;
overflow:hidden}` + only `#stratBody{flex:1;overflow-y:auto}` scrolling meant anything
outside `#stratBody` just got clipped once it exceeded the remaining vertical space —
no scrollbar appeared at all past wherever the clip landed (right around the Confluence
Tags heading, matching Kev's report exactly).

WHAT CHANGED:
- 6th tab "📖 Learn" after Raw Log. The whole Glossary is now `.stratPane[data-spane=
  "learn"]` — a sibling of the other 5 panes, inheriting the SAME working
  `overflow-y:auto` they already use. No new scroll mechanism invented; reused the one
  that was already correct everywhere else.
- Learning Mode toggle DELETED — button, CSS, and all its JS
  (`_learningModeOn`/`_applyLearningMode`/`_toggleLearningMode`, the tap-popup
  position/clamp math, the document-level close-on-click-elsewhere listener). Confirmed
  zero remaining references to any of these identifiers anywhere in the file.
- (i) icons: always visible now (removed the `display:none`/`.learningModeOn`-gated CSS),
  in every pane they already existed in, PLUS one new icon added to Indicator Scoreboard's
  label (PHASE 18 shipped without one).
- New "🗺️ Sections" list at the top of the Learn pane — 16 entries in on-page order
  (Scorecard, Equity Curve, Setup Volume Heatmap; Funnel, Skip/Reject Reasons, Shadow
  Outcomes, Gate Scoreboard, Shadow Tag Leaderboard, Shadow Combo Leaderboard, Weekly
  Regret Trend; Win Rate by Grade, Tag Leaderboard, Combo Leaderboard, Planned R:R
  Distribution, System Over Time, Indicator Scoreboard) — each a stable `id="learnEntry-
  <key>"` div. All 16 texts reused verbatim from PHASE 17's `SECTION_TOOLTIPS`; only
  Indicator Scoreboard's is new copy (drafted and confirmed with Kev before writing):
  "The Indicator Scoreboard lines up every confluence tool in one table: its hand-set
  Points, its real win rate on actual closed trades, a week-by-week trend of that win
  rate, and — where it exists — the same tool's hypothetical (shadow) win rate on setups
  nobody took. Sort any column by tapping its header; rows with fewer than 3 closed
  trades are dimmed, not hidden."
- Concept Glossary (6 concepts) and Tag Glossary (123 tags, search box unchanged) sit
  below Sections — moved as-is, only the shared row class renamed `glossaryEntry` →
  `learnEntry` (all three lists now share one consistent look).
- Deep-link behavior: clicking any (i) icon → `_switchStratTab('learn')` (the SAME
  function the tab-click handler itself now calls, extracted once so both paths can't
  drift apart) → `scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'})` on the matching `#learnEntry-<key>`
  (finds `#stratBody`'s scrolling ancestor automatically) → a 1.8s `.justJumped` violet
  flash (restarted via a forced reflow — `void entry.offsetWidth` — if the same entry is
  jumped to twice in a row, so the highlight is visibly obvious every time, not just once).

VERIFICATION: `node -e` syntax check on both inline `<script>` blocks — clean. `<div>`
balance 579/579. Cross-match of `SECTION_TOOLTIPS` keys / `SECTION_ORDER` keys / every
`data-learn` attribute in the markup — 16/16/16, exact, no orphans. Grep confirmed zero
remaining references to every deleted identifier. No Python touched — no restart needed.

KEV VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (verbatim, per STEP 3 — not yet run by Claude, needs a browser):
1. Learn tab opens and scrolls all the way to the bottom of the tag glossary, on both
   desktop and phone.
2. Every (i) icon in every pane jumps to the right Learn entry and visibly flashes it.
3. Glossary search still filters the Confluence Tags list correctly.
4. No toggle button anywhere in the header.
5. Every other tab is pixel-equivalent to before this phase.
6. Deploy via `push_dashboard.py`, re-check on phone.

## INDICATOR SCOREBOARD (PHASE 18, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: Kev's own requested chart — every tool with its score, AND visible proof
of whether each tool is earning trust over time. Points are deliberately static (hand-set
by Kev); win rates are what the automation updates — the sparkline is where improvement
actually shows.

BACKEND: `GET /api/strategy/tag_trends?all=0|1` — see the banner above for the full
discovery/implementation summary. Route lives in dexter.py right after `/api/tag_registry`.
Schema: `{"all": bool, "since": "YYYY-MM-DD"|null, "tags": {code: [{"week", "wr", "n"}, ...]},
"cache_age_secs": float}`. `since` is null when `?all=1` (no era filter applied) or if
`SYSTEM_ERA`'s date suffix ever fails to parse (fails open — full history, not a crash).

FRONTEND: `#stratScoreboardTable` in the Performance pane, after PHASE 13's System Over
Time charts. `loadScoreboard()` added to `loadAll()`'s existing `Promise.all([...])` —
rides the Strategy overlay's normal 25s refresh, no new polling loop. Deliberately fetches
`/api/strategy/performance` and `/api/strategy/counterfactual` independently rather than
sharing `loadPerformance()`/`loadShadow()`'s in-flight requests for the same endpoints —
a small duplicate-request cost per 25s cycle, accepted because `/api/strategy/performance`
has no server cache and recomputes cheaply (the journal is under 100 entries today); the
alternative (coordinating shared state across concurrent Promise.all branches) added
complexity for a saving that won't matter until the journal is orders of magnitude bigger.
Column-header clicks (`th[data-sort]`) toggle `_scoreboardSort {col, dir}` and re-render;
nulls (a tag with no real trades, or no shadow data, or no CONFLUENCE_SCORES match) always
sort to the bottom regardless of ascending/descending.

KEV VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (verbatim, per STEP 4 — not yet run by Claude, needs a live
restart + browser):
1. Numbers in the Real WR column must match the existing Tag Leaderboard EXACTLY (same
   source field) — any mismatch is a bug, stop and report if you see one.
2. Sparklines will be sparse this early (most tags have few or zero closed trades since
   the PHASE 11 era boundary) — that's honest, not broken.
3. Click each sortable column header, confirm ascending/descending toggles and nulls
   consistently sort last.
4. Mobile: confirm the table scrolls horizontally inside its own wrapper without
   affecting the rest of the panel at a narrow viewport.
5. Console clean; deploy via `push_dashboard.py`, re-check on phone.

================================================================================
## LEARNING MODE: ⓘ TOOLTIPS + GLOSSARY (PHASE 17, 2026-07-07, DEPLOY REQUIRED, NO RESTART)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: the board should teach its reader. Tooltips carry the one-liners;
anything longer lives in the Glossary so bubbles never become essays.

FULL SECTION TOOLTIP TEXT (`SECTION_TOOLTIPS` in webapp/index.html, one per
`data-learn` key):

- scorecard: Your all-time paper-trading track record across every closed trade Chev has
  posted: win rate, profit factor, expectancy per trade, how many trades have closed, and
  net P&L. Real performance on the paper account, not a projection — but it's all-time, so
  a rough early stretch can still weigh on the numbers long after the system has improved.
- equity_curve: A running total of profit and loss after every closed trade, plotted over
  time. Each point is the cumulative P&L up to that trade's close.
- setup_volume_heatmap: How many setups Dexter has evaluated by day of week and hour of
  day (UTC), over the last 14 days — whether or not they were ever escalated to Chev.
- funnel: Every 2 minutes Dexter scans the watchlist. This counts how many setups he saw,
  how many were filtered out before Chev ever saw them, how many he sent to Chev, what
  Chev decided, and how many survived George's risk checks to actually open — last 24h.
- skip_reject_reasons: A breakdown of exactly why setups didn't become trades in the last
  24 hours — Chev's own skip reasoning, or which specific gate/gauntlet check rejected it.
- shadow_outcomes: What would have happened, hypothetically, to setups that were skipped
  or rejected — bullets dodged vs. money left on the table, realistic costs modelled in.
  Hypothetical numbers for tuning the system, never merged into real performance stats.
- gate_scoreboard: Breaks the shadow outcomes down by exactly which gate rejected the
  setup, showing each gate's own hypothetical win rate and R.
- shadow_tag_leaderboard: Hypothetical win rate per confluence tag, skipped/killed setups
  only — a much larger sample than real trades, but not a random one (Chev skipped them
  for a reason) — leads for review, not proof.
- shadow_combo_leaderboard: Same idea one level more specific — the exact combination of
  tags, not one at a time. Below-trust-minimum combos shown greyed out.
- weekly_regret_trend: Hypothetical profit "left on the table" by skipped/rejected setups,
  totalled per week, full history. A shrinking trend suggests the system is improving.
- win_rate_by_grade: Real win rate on closed trades, grouped by the quality grade (B/A/A+)
  assigned when the setup was first evaluated.
- tag_leaderboard: Real win rate on CLOSED trades, one row per tag Chev cited when he
  posted — actual money-on-the-line performance, rows need 3+ closed trades to show.
- combo_leaderboard: Same real win-rate idea, one level more specific — the exact set of
  tags cited together. Sample sizes are thin (mostly 1-2 trades), below-trust rows greyed.
- planned_rr_distribution: A histogram of the Risk:Reward Dexter actually calculated at
  entry time — George's real cost-adjusted formula, not a rough estimate.
- system_over_time: Three charts tracking how the system's own rules have moved over
  time, with markers for every restart/settings change — R:R pressure, threshold vs flow,
  and stop-distance reality. For spotting whether a tuning change helped, not judging one trade.

CONCEPT GLOSSARY (`CONCEPT_GLOSSARY`, 6 entries, name/definition/how):
1. Confluence Score — Dexter's own summed indicator points; a setup must clear a minimum
   before Chev ever sees it.
2. Risk:Reward (R:R) — target distance ÷ stop distance from entry.
3. Net R:R — the SAME ratio adjusted for real round-trip cost: `(reward% − cost%) ÷
   (risk% + cost%)`. The number George actually enforces, not the raw R:R.
4. Shadow Outcomes — hypothetical win/loss results for skipped/rejected setups, same
   triple-barrier method as real trades, never touching real stats.
5. Setup Grades (B/A/A+) — score-ratio-based tier, boosted by trend/peak-session, reduced
   for low-session forex. No "C" grade exists in the code — flagged explicitly.
6. The Funnel Stages — seen → filtered pre-escalation → escalated to Chev → Chev's
   verdict → George's gate/gauntlet checks → opened.

KEV VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (verbatim, per STEP 4 — not yet run by Claude, needs a
browser):
1. Toggle ON → ⓘ appears next to all 15 section labels across every Strategy tab; tap
   opens a readable popup; tap elsewhere (or a different icon) closes/replaces it;
   Glossary appears below the tabs with all concepts + all registry tags, search filters.
2. Toggle OFF → pixel-identical to before this phase (no icons, no Glossary, no header
   change beyond the small 🎓 button itself).
3. Reload the page → the toggle's last state is remembered (localStorage).
4. Confirm nothing outside the Strategy panel changed.
5. Console clean; deploy via `push_dashboard.py`, re-check on phone (popup stays inside
   the viewport at narrow widths).

================================================================================
## TAG REGISTRY + FRIENDLY NAMES EVERYWHERE (PHASE 16, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: the board currently speaks in code words; the registry makes it speak
English — and becomes the single source of truth PHASEs 17/18 render from. One correction
lives in one place.

DISCOVERY — STOP-CHECKED with Kev before writing any names (per this phase's own STEP 1):
- Tag codes come from THREE vocabularies, not one:
  1. `CONFLUENCE_SCORES` (dexter.py, ANCHOR `"gp": 4,`) — 77 keys, Dexter's real weights
     table, the source `points` is read from.
  2. Chev's own free-typed `tags=` field (parsed `dexter.py:7584`, stored on closed
     trades) — 44 distinct codes actually observed in chev_journal.json, a superset of #1
     plus 8 with no weights-table match at all: `bb_squeeze`/`bbsq`/`bbsqueeze` (three
     spellings of the same thing), `ema_5m`/`fib_5m` (a timeframe not in the weights
     table), `hd`/`rd` (inferred shorthand, unconfirmed), `tp_balance_extreme` (unclear
     origin, unconfirmed).
  3. `labeller.py`'s `normalize_reasons()` tokens (`REASON_MAP_ORDERED` + `sr_multi`/
     `sr_single` + 4 `pattern_*` + `other`) — 42 distinct, used ONLY by the PHASE 7B-3
     Shadow Tag/Combo leaderboards. A differently-shaped vocabulary (percentage-based Fib
     levels: `fib_50`/`fib_618`/etc.; no-underscore EMA periods: `ema55`/`ema21`/`ema13`)
     that mostly does NOT string-match the weights table — only `gp`/`rsi_ob`/`rsi_os`
     match exactly.
- Union: 123 unique codes. Verified by exact set comparison against a fresh read of
  chev_journal.json — nothing guessed that doesn't exist, nothing in the registry that
  isn't observed somewhere.
- Kev's confirmed handling for the two ambiguous cases: `points: null` for any code
  without an EXACT `CONFLUENCE_SCORES` match — no alias table between differently-spelled
  versions of the same concept (simplest, safest, nothing to keep in sync by hand as new
  tags appear). `hd`/`rd` are labeled in their own tooltip as an inferred, unconfirmed
  reading ("Hidden Divergence"/"Regular Divergence" shorthand) rather than asserted as fact.
- Frontend render sites confirmed: `#stratTagBars` (Tag Leaderboard), `#stratComboBars`
  (Combo Leaderboard), and the single `renderShadowLeaderboard()` function that serves
  BOTH `#stratShadowTagBars` and `#stratShadowComboBars` (PHASE 7B-3). Two more tag-code
  render sites exist (Chev's Corner ideas panel tag chips, the hypothetical-trade-card
  component) but sit OUTSIDE the Strategy section — left untouched per this phase's own
  scope; flagged here for a future phase if Kev wants them covered too.

IMPLEMENTATION:
- `dexter.py`: new `TAG_REGISTRY` dict (ANCHOR: immediately after `CONFLUENCE_SCORES`'s
  closing brace) — one entry per code with `name`/`tooltip`/`definition`/`how`. Written
  from reading the actual computing code wherever mechanics weren't obvious: Golden Pocket
  is the REAL code's 50%-61.8% Fib band (not quite the `CONFLUENCE_SCORES` comment's
  "0.618-0.65" phrasing — the comment was slightly off from what the code actually does);
  a liquidity sweep is a wick through a cluster of equal highs/lows within ~40 candles that
  closes back inside (`_detect_liquidity_sweep`); `sr_multi`/`sr_single` is a 3+-touch
  threshold read straight from `labeller.py`'s own regex. Deliberately NO `points` field
  stored on the dict — new `GET /api/tag_registry` (300s cache; tag meanings only change
  when this file is edited, never at runtime, so a long cache is safe) looks up `points`
  fresh from `CONFLUENCE_SCORES` on every serve — retuning a weight in code is
  automatically reflected on the site, nothing hardcoded twice.
- `webapp/index.html`: shared `friendlyTag(code)` / `friendlyCombo(comboKey)` (comma-
  joined combo keys split, each piece mapped, joined with " + ", e.g. "Golden Pocket + EMA
  55 + RSI Divergence (4H)"). `_loadTagRegistry()` fetches once per page load (module-level
  cache, kicked off in the same init block as `loadVitals()`; also raced in parallel via
  `Promise.all` at the top of `loadPerformance()`/`loadShadow()` so a first-ever open can
  never show the raw-code fallback). Unknown codes fall back to a plain prettifier
  (underscores → spaces, capitalized) — never breaks on a brand-new tag. Applied at all
  three confirmed render sites; every row's `title` attribute still shows the raw code
  unchanged, for cross-referencing logs.

VERIFICATION: extract-and-exec (no `import dexter`) — 9/9 assertions: every one of the 44
distinct tags actually in chev_journal.json resolves to a registry name (0 missing), every
one of the 77 `CONFLUENCE_SCORES` keys resolves to a registry name, a matching code serves
its real point value (`gp` → 4), a non-matching code serves `points: null` (`bbsq`), the
300s cache is exercised, and retuning `CONFLUENCE_SCORES['gp']` live is proven to flow
through to the very next serve (99) — proof `points` is never hardcoded twice. `python -m
py_compile dexter.py` clean. `node -e` syntax check on both inline `<script>` blocks —
clean. `<div>` tag balance — 557/557, unchanged (label text only, no markup added/removed).

## TUNABLES.JSON HOT-RELOAD (PHASE 14, 2026-07-07, RESTART REQUIRED ONCE, NO DEPLOY)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: PHASE 15 (web tuning) needs settings that can change without a restart,
and bounds enforcement has to live server-side — the site is a remote control, never the
authority. Bounds are the guarantee that no fat finger, bug, or 2am impulse can set a
threshold to zero.

DISCOVERY — STOP-CHECKED with Kev before any edit (per this phase's own STEP 1):
- Every proposed key confirmed read fresh per-cycle/per-call, nowhere baked into a
  module-level structure at import time:
  - `CONFLUENCE_THRESHOLD_{CRYPTO,FOREX,STOCK}`, `EXPLORATION_THRESHOLD_{CRYPTO,FOREX,
    STOCK}`, `ESCALATION_MAX_DIST_PCT`, `EXPLORATION_MAX_DIST_PCT` — plain globals, read
    exclusively via `_active_thresholds(asset_type)` (dexter.py), a pure per-call function.
  - `ESCALATION_TF_FLOOR` (dict) — read per-setup inside the main loop, compared against
    the fixed `TF_SECONDS` dict (bounds = "must be a TF_SECONDS key", not a numeric range).
  - `HALLUCINATION_MAX_ENTRY_DIST` — plain global, read per-setup inside the main loop.
  - risk_gauntlet.py's `_EXPLORATION["MIN_NET_RR"/"MAX_COST_R"/"CONCURRENCY_CAP"]` — every
    `get_active_profile()` caller (7 call sites across both files, including the
    EXECUTABLE GEOMETRY block builder and the fill-time re-validation path) holds a live
    reference to the same dict object, so in-place mutation propagates everywhere
    immediately with zero additional wiring.
- No key needed a refactor or exclusion — a clean, all-safe discovery result.
- Kev's scope decisions, on record: whitelist stays EXACTLY as originally proposed, no
  wider. `_NORMAL` stays untouchable — it's the "return to discipline" baseline and only
  means something as a fixed reference point; a driftable baseline makes "restore
  defaults" circular. `ABS_MIN_RR` (hard safety backstop), `MAX_TOTAL_HEAT`/
  `MAX_CORR_SAME_DIR` (account-protection, already on the global do-not-touch list), and
  `ATR_FLOOR` (feeds the EXECUTABLE GEOMETRY coaching block — more coupling than a
  first-round tunable should carry) all stay OUT on purpose. Expand later, one key at a
  time, only when actually needed — never because it was easy.

IMPLEMENTATION:
- `risk_gauntlet.py`: new `EXPLORATION_TUNABLE_KEYS = {"MIN_NET_RR", "MAX_COST_R",
  "CONCURRENCY_CAP"}` and new public `apply_exploration_overrides(updates)` — the ONLY
  sanctioned way to mutate `_EXPLORATION` from outside this module. Mutates in place.
  Refuses (skips, warns) any key outside `EXPLORATION_TUNABLE_KEYS`, any unknown
  trade_type, any non-numeric value — a second, independent lock behind dexter.py's own
  bounds check ("two doors, both locked"), per Kev's explicit condition. Has NO mode
  parameter — it is physically incapable of touching `_NORMAL`, by construction, not by a
  runtime check. Returns exactly what was applied (never the full profile) so the caller
  can diff/log precisely. 5 new self-test cases (27–31): valid override applied +
  restored; non-whitelisted key (`ATR_FLOOR`) refused; unknown trade_type refused;
  non-numeric value refused; `_NORMAL` proven untouched across all of the above. Self-test
  suite: 33/33 passing (up from 26).
- `dexter.py`: new `TUNABLES_FILE = r"C:\ChevTools\tunables.json"`, `TUNABLES_BOUNDS`
  (dotted-path → (min, max), full table + rationale in a comment block directly above it
  in the source), and `load_tunables()` — called once per scan cycle, the very first line
  inside `while True:` (before the Firebase balance/win-stats refresh that already lived
  there). Reads the file, validates every present key, applies only in-bounds AND
  actually-different values, and records the full diff to the flight recorder via
  `record_system_state("tunables_applied", "file", changed={...})`. Escalation-threshold/
  TF-floor/hallucination-guard keys are reassigned directly (`global`, same module);
  exploration-profile keys go through `risk_gauntlet.apply_exploration_overrides()`.
  File missing → silent no-op (the normal pre-tuning state, not an error). File corrupt,
  or any single value out of bounds/malformed/an unrecognized key → warned ONCE (a module-
  level flag prevents spamming every 2-minute cycle) and that value's last-good stays in
  force; a bad value never blocks its unrelated siblings from applying in the same cycle.
- Shipped `C:\ChevTools\tunables.json` containing exactly today's hardcoded live values —
  deliberately a no-op on first read (see the banner's BEHAVIOR NOTE for why a real diff
  only shows up once Kev actually edits a value and restarts).

FULL WHITELIST + BOUNDS (JSON path → allowed range/set):
  escalation_thresholds.normal.score.crypto        (1, 20)      [currently 10]
  escalation_thresholds.normal.score.forex         (1, 20)      [currently 8]
  escalation_thresholds.normal.score.stock         (1, 20)      [currently 8]
  escalation_thresholds.normal.max_dist_pct        (0.1, 5.0)   [currently 0.75]

## TIME-SERIES CHARTS + THE ANNOTATION LAYER (PHASE 13, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: three of the biggest open questions (when to re-enable EV; did each
tuning help; did the coaching land) previously required log-mining by hand. These three
charts convert them into glances.

DISCOVERY (done before any edit, per rule 4/STEP 1):
- Equity Curve (ANCHOR `📈 Equity Curve`, `renderEquityCurve()`) renders via
  `LightweightCharts.createChart()` — the SAME library already loaded globally from
  `cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/lightweight-charts@4.1.3` (confirmed the exact pinned build
  really does expose `LineType.WithSteps` before using it, by fetching and inspecting
  the actual CDN bundle rather than assuming). Reused directly; no new library added.
  Lazy-init-then-`setData()`-on-every-refresh is the established pattern, followed here.
- *** CRITICAL FINDING, reported loudly in the top banner too: `system_state.jsonl`
  (PHASE 10) does not exist on disk, and NOT ONE line in chev_decisions.jsonl
  (2,739 lines checked) carries any PHASE 11 structured field — Dexter has not been
  restarted since those phases landed in source. Both are fully implemented and
  verified in code; neither has ever run live. Every chart in this phase will show its
  empty-state fallback until Kev restarts Dexter (again) after this phase too. ***
- Performance tab body (`data-spane="performance"`) ends right after `#stratRHist` —
  the new section is inserted there, "below the existing Performance content" per spec.

BACKEND (dexter.py): new `GET /api/strategy/timeseries?days=N` (default 30), 300s
module-level cache KEYED ON `days` (so a different window never serves another window's
stale cache) — same cache shape as PHASE 7B-1/12. Reads `chev_decisions.jsonl` once,
buckets by calendar day (UTC, matching how every ts in this codebase is already written):
  - `rr_pressure`: per day, median `enforced_rr_floor`, median `ev_advisory_rr`, and
    median/min/max of `planned_rr` (the min/max become the "band" the frontend draws as
    two dashed lines either side of the median — LightweightCharts v4 has no native
    fill-between-two-lines primitive, so this is the honest simple version, not a new
    dependency).
  - `flow`: count of all decisions that day (`escalations`) and count where
    `decision == "POST"` (`posts`).
  - `stop_reality`: median/P10/P90 of `stop_pct` on POST or any `*REJECT` decision that day.
  - `threshold` + `annotations`: read from `system_state.jsonl` separately (sparse,
    event-driven — reported as-is, no day-forcing/interpolation server-side; the frontend
    plots them on their own real timestamps, letting LightweightCharts merge time axes).
    `threshold.score` = `snapshot.escalation_thresholds.active.crypto.score` (crypto
    chosen as the representative asset — forex/stock threshold history is in the same
    snapshot if a future phase wants a per-asset toggle). `annotations[].summary` =
    `"key: old→new"` joined by `"; "` when `changed` is set, else the bare `event` name
    (e.g. `"startup"`).
  - `earliest_structured_ts`: earliest timestamp ANYWHERE in the log (not windowed by
    `days`) carrying any of `planned_rr`/`ev_advisory_rr`/`enforced_rr_floor`/`stop_pct` —
    drives the frontend's "collecting data since…" message. Currently null (see finding
    above) — that is the correct, honest value, not a bug.
  - `crypto_day_cost_floor_pct`: `2 × (FEE_SIDE["crypto"] + SLIPPAGE_SIDE["crypto"]) × 100`
    = 0.14 today — a stop tighter than this (in the same percent units as `stop_pct`)
    can't clear round-trip costs even on a full winner; drawn as a dashed horizontal
    `createPriceLine()` on the stop-distance chart, PHASE 2's COST GATE made visual.
  Verified via extract-and-exec (no `import dexter`) against a `tempfile.TemporaryDirectory()`
  fixture — 17/17 assertions passed, including day-bucketing, median/min/max math, the
  earliest-structured-ts exclusion of pre-PHASE-11 entries, annotation summary formatting,
  the cost-floor arithmetic, and the days-keyed cache (same `days` reuses cache;
  different `days` recomputes rather than serving a stale window). `python -m py_compile
  dexter.py` clean.

FRONTEND (webapp/index.html): new "📉 System Over Time" section (`#tsChartsWrap`, three
`.tsChart` divs — `#tsRrChart`/`#tsFlowChart`/`#tsStopChart` — plus a single
`#tsEmptyNote` fallback) inserted after `#stratRHist`, still inside the Performance pane.
`loadTimeseries()` folded into the EXISTING `loadAll()` `Promise.all([...])` (now includes
it alongside `loadMode`/`loadFeed`/`loadFunnel`/`loadPerformance`/`loadHeatmap`/`loadShadow`)
— rides the Strategy overlay's existing 25s refresh and PHASE 12's `_markFresh('strategy')`
stamp; no second polling loop introduced.
  - R:R Pressure chart: enforced floor (red step line), EV-advisory (blue line), Chev's
    proposals (gold median line + grey dashed min/max band).
  - Threshold vs Flow chart: escalation-score threshold (gold step line, left price
    scale), escalations/day (grey histogram, right scale), surviving POSTs/day (green
    line, right scale) — two price scales so counts and the threshold number don't
    fight for the same axis.
  - Stop-Distance Reality chart: median `stop_pct` (gold line) + grey dashed P10/P90
    band, with the crypto day-trade cost floor as a dashed red horizontal price line.
  - Annotation markers (`series.setMarkers()`) placed on whichever chart's own day-bucket
    matches an event's date — an event landing on a day with no bucket in a PARTICULAR
    chart's data simply isn't markable on THAT chart (no synthetic bucket invented); it
    can still appear on another chart whose data does cover that day.
  - Empty state: `_tsHasData()` checks for any real value across `rr_pressure`/
    `threshold`; if none, `#tsChartsWrap` hides and `#tsEmptyNote` shows either
    "Collecting data since `<earliest_structured_ts>`…" or, if that's null too (today's
    actual state), "No structured data yet — appears after Dexter's next restart."
  - `node -e` syntax check on both extracted inline `<script>` blocks — clean.
    `<div>`/`</div>` balance — 557 opens / 557 closes, balanced.

## STRUCTURED DECISION LOGGING (PHASE 11, 2026-07-07, RESTART REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: the dashboard's reason bars and the counterfactual audit both had to
regex-mine Chev's/the gauntlet's own PROSE ("Round-trip cost 0.35R... exceeds max 0.25R")
to recover numbers the system had already computed exactly, as floats, upstream. This
makes those numbers first-class JSON fields so future charts (Phase 13) and audits are
one-line queries instead of string-parsing exercises.

DISCOVERY:
  (a) `_log_chev_decision` (dexter.py, ANCHOR unchanged) has exactly 10 call sites,
      classified by decision type:
        HALLUCINATED_LEVELS reject (decision="REJECT", Phase 6's hallucination guard)
        GATE_REJECT      (SCORE GATE)
        STRUCT_REJECT    (structural prerequisite)
        MTF_TAX_REJECT   (counter-trend confidence tax)
        GEOMETRY_REJECT  (ATR/R:R/size pre-check, after a failed one-retry revision)
        REJECT (x2)      (risk_gauntlet.run_gauntlet(), fixable-retry-failed AND
                           not-fixable branches — both use decision="REJECT")
        POST             (trade actually locked)
        FORMAT_ERROR     (Chev's reply matched neither POST: nor SKIP:)
        SKIP             (Chev's own judgment call)
      At every one of the first 7 (all POST/REJECT-family), the code path logs BEFORE
      nulling `parsed["trade"]`, confirmed by reading each site directly — so Chev's
      proposed entry/sl/tp are still in scope at the moment of the log call, with no
      extra plumbing needed to keep them alive.
  (b) The gauntlet call (ANCHOR: `_g_res = risk_gauntlet.run_gauntlet(`) returns a dict
      whose PASS branch already exposed `sized["cost_R"]` (existing, untouched), but the
      EV number computed at gate 8 (`ev_required_rr`, inside the NET_RR gate's `if
      eligible:` branch) only ever existed baked into a prose string (`ev_advisory_note`,
      exploration-mode only) — confirmed by reading gate 8 directly. `_reject()` (the
      helper every REJECT path returns through) had no mechanism to carry these numbers
      out on a REJECT verdict at all. Fixed at the source (risk_gauntlet.py), not by
      re-deriving the numbers in dexter.py — see THE CHANGE below.
  (c) Confirmed 3 real consumers of chev_decisions.jsonl, all tolerant of unknown/additive
      fields (checked by reading each): dexter.py's `api_strategy_feed()` and
      `api_strategy_funnel()` (both read via `.get()` accessors only, `api_strategy_feed`
      returns whole records including any new fields — harmless, nothing renders them
      yet); `counterfactual_report.py`'s `_load_jsonl()` (generic `json.loads()` per line,
      reads only `ts`/`decision`/`reason` — see PHASE 7 — ignores everything else).
      webapp/index.html's `renderFeed()`/`renderRawTable()` (plain JS property reads,
      `undefined` on a missing key, never throws). No consumer enumerates or validates a
      fixed field set anywhere — safe to add fields freely.

THE CHANGE:
  - risk_gauntlet.py: `_reject(code, reason, fixable=False, cost_r=None,
    ev_advisory_rr=None, enforced_rr_floor=None)` — 3 new optional kwargs, defaulting to
    None so every EARLIER reject (equity/side-sanity/data-quality/stale-price/ATR-floor)
    and every LATER one (liquidation/heat/corr/concurrency) is completely untouched and
    correctly carries None (those numbers genuinely don't exist yet/aren't relevant at
    those gates). Only the COST_GATE reject (gate 7) passes `cost_r`; only the NET_RR
    reject (gate 8) passes all three (`ev_advisory_rr` only when `eligible` tags exist,
    else None — never guessed). The PASS return dict gained the same 3 keys at the top
    level (alongside the pre-existing, UNCHANGED `sized["cost_R"]`/`sized["net_rr"]`).
    `ev_advisory_rr` is exposed whenever the EV number is computed, REGARDLESS of
    exploration_mode — a small, deliberate improvement over today's notes-string, which
    only ever narrates it in the exploration-advisory case; the raw float now exists on
    the return dict in both modes, giving MORE visibility than before, not just parity.
  - dexter.py: new `_trade_metrics_for_log(parsed)` — pure, computes `planned_rr` (gross
    reward-distance / risk-distance ratio, NOT the gauntlet's cost-adjusted `net_rr`),
    `stop_pct`/`tp_pct` (REAL PERCENTAGE NUMBERS, e.g. 1.622 meaning 1.622% — not the
    fraction 0.01622 — so "rounded to 4 decimals" keeps genuine precision on tight stops
    instead of collapsing to 2 decimal digits of percent), and `trade_type_chosen`,
    directly from Chev's own parsed TRADE: line. Independent of whether the gauntlet ever
    ran, so it's available at all 7 POST/REJECT-family sites uniformly, including the 4
    that reject BEFORE risk_gauntlet.run_gauntlet() is ever called. Returns all-None,
    never raises, if no usable trade/entry/sl/tp is present.
  - `_log_chev_decision()` signature extended with 8 new optional kwargs (all default
    None): `planned_rr, stop_pct, tp_pct, cost_r, trade_type_chosen, ev_advisory_rr,
    enforced_rr_floor, deliberation_secs` — appended to the JSON entry dict unconditionally
    (present as keys on every decision, null when not applicable — matches "all fields
    additive; absent = null" literally, not "field missing entirely").
  - New `_esc_start_ts = time.time()` captured immediately before the FIRST
    `ask_chev_to_judge(...)` call for an escalation — `deliberation_secs =
    round(time.time() - _esc_start_ts, 1)` computed fresh at each log call, so it
    naturally accumulates across any hallucination/geometry/gauntlet retries within the
    same escalation, not just the first round-trip.
  - Wired at 9 of the 10 call sites: full trade metrics + deliberation_secs at the 5
    upstream rejects (HALLUCINATED_LEVELS/GATE_REJECT/STRUCT_REJECT/MTF_TAX_REJECT/
    GEOMETRY_REJECT); trade metrics + gauntlet fields (`cost_r`/`ev_advisory_rr`/
    `enforced_rr_floor` read from `_g_res`) + deliberation_secs at the 2 gauntlet REJECT
    sites and POST; deliberation_secs only at FORMAT_ERROR. SKIP's call site is completely
    untouched — see the ambiguity flag in the top banner for why.

VERIFICATION DONE: `python -m py_compile dexter.py risk_gauntlet.py` clean.
`python -X utf8 risk_gauntlet.py` — grew from 25 to 28 cases (24b/25b: structured fields
correct on both the exploration-PASS and non-exploration-REJECT poisoned-tag fixtures,
confirming `ev_advisory_rr` is the same 4.60 in both modes while `enforced_rr_floor`
correctly differs (1.2 flat floor vs 4.60 enforced EV); 26: an early NO_EQUITY reject

run_gauntlet()` call, not invented numbers) alongside every original field unchanged, and

## THE FLIGHT RECORDER: system_state.jsonl (PHASE 10, 2026-07-07, RESTART REQUIRED)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: every gate decision gets logged (chev_decisions.jsonl, labels_*.jsonl),
but the RULES that produced those decisions never did — the July drought's timeline had
to be reconstructed from handoff prose, checkpoint by checkpoint. This is the black-box
recorder: it makes thresholds chartable (future phase), changes attributable, and "did
that tweak actually help?" answerable from data instead of memory. Trader logic: you
journal your trades; this journals your rules.

DISCOVERY — full tunable inventory + locations (nothing guessed; every value read fresh):
  dexter.py:
    - Escalation thresholds: `_active_thresholds(asset_type)` (ANCHOR, unchanged this
      phase) resolves the LIVE score/max_dist_pct per asset type from six underlying
      constants: `CONFLUENCE_THRESHOLD_CRYPTO/FOREX/STOCK` + `ESCALATION_MAX_DIST_PCT`
      (normal), `EXPLORATION_THRESHOLD_CRYPTO/FOREX/STOCK` + `EXPLORATION_MAX_DIST_PCT`
      (exploration). Snapshot captures all three views: the resolved "active" value per
      asset type (what's actually in force right now) AND the raw normal/exploration
      tables (so a regime you're NOT currently in is still visible for comparison).
    - `EXPLORATION_MODE` (bool), `ESCALATION_TF_FLOOR` (dict), `SYSTEM_ERA` (string),
      `HALLUCINATION_MAX_ENTRY_DIST` / `HALLUCINATION_MAX_SLTP_DIST` (Phase 6),
      `TRADE_TYPE_EXPIRY_HOURS`, `MAX_LEVERAGE_BY_TYPE` — all read directly, all exactly
      as named in the phase's own minimum list (plus TRADE_TYPE_EXPIRY_HOURS/
      MAX_LEVERAGE_BY_TYPE, immediately adjacent to the named constants and clearly
      "tunable" in the same sense — flagged here rather than silently included).
  risk_gauntlet.py:
    - Both setup-quality profiles (`_NORMAL`/`_EXPLORATION`) captured WHOLE, via the
      existing PUBLIC accessor `risk_gauntlet.get_active_profile(True/False)` — never the
      private `_NORMAL`/`_EXPLORATION` names directly. This automatically includes every
      key in each profile (`ATR_FLOOR`, `MAX_COST_R`, `MIN_NET_RR`, `ABS_MIN_RR`,
      `MAX_TOTAL_HEAT`, `MAX_CORR_SAME_DIR`, `CONCURRENCY_CAP`) — a deliberate choice over
      cherry-picking the phase's named subset (MIN_NET_RR/MAX_COST_R/ATR_FLOOR/
      concurrency/heat), since capturing the whole dict means a future new profile key
      is captured automatically with no edit to this phase's code, and ABS_MIN_RR/
      MAX_CORR_SAME_DIR sitting right next to the named keys in the SAME dict would have
      been an odd, easy-to-miss omission otherwise.
    - Mode-independent constants, read directly: `FEE_SIDE`, `SLIPPAGE_SIDE`,
      `FUNDING_EST_SWING`, `EV_SAFETY_MARGIN`, `MIN_SAMPLES_FOR_EV`,
      `TAG_WINRATE_WINDOW_TRADES`, `TAG_WINRATE_SMOOTHING_K` — exactly the phase's named
      list, nothing more. Deliberately did NOT include the true account-safety constants
      (`MIN_EQUITY`, `LIQ_SAFETY`, `MAX_MARGIN_PCT`, `ATR_SANITY_BAND`,
      `STALE_PRICE_FRAC`, `RISK_BANDS`, `LEV_CAPS`) — these never move regardless of mode
      and aren't part of "what changed" in the sense this recorder exists to track; they're
      also explicitly the DO-NOT-TOUCH account-safety gates this phase (and every phase)
      must leave alone. Flagged here rather than silently omitted.

THE CHANGE — dexter.py only (no other file touched):
  - New constant `SYSTEM_STATE_FILE = r"C:\ChevTools\system_state.jsonl"`.
  - New `snapshot_tunables()` (pure, read-only, no side effects) — assembles the full
    inventory above into one dict, JSON-serializable end to end.
  - New `record_system_state(event, source, changed=None)` — appends exactly one JSON
    line (`{ts, event, source, system_era, exploration_mode, snapshot, changed}`) via
    plain file append (`"a"` mode, never `"w"`, never rewrites prior lines). Wrapped in a
    try/except that logs `[system_state] record_system_state failed (...)` and returns
    silently on any failure (disk full, locked file, permissions) — this is a pure
    observability side-channel, must never be able to crash the scan loop, and never
    reads its own file back (no feedback into any gate/decision path).
  - Both new functions placed right after `check_and_update_open_trades()`, immediately
    before the "MAIN LOOP" section header — next to their primary call site, not buried
    in the constants block far above.
  - Call site 1 (startup): `record_system_state("startup", "startup")` placed
    immediately after `print("Dexter is watching the markets...")`, BEFORE the Google
    Sheets connection attempt (which retries and can fail) — so a crash-loop restart
    still gets one recorded snapshot even if everything after it falls over.
  - Call site 2 (toggle): inside `api_strategy_toggle_exploration()` (ANCHOR:
    `toggle_exploration`) — captures `_old_mode` before flipping `EXPLORATION_MODE`,
    then calls `record_system_state("toggle", "web", changed={"exploration_mode":
    {"old": _old_mode, "new": EXPLORATION_MODE}})` right after the flip.
  - Step 3's "one reusable function any future change-path calls" is satisfied by
    `record_system_state`'s generic signature (`event`, `source`, `changed=None`) — no
    other call sites were added beyond the two specified; future phases can call it
    directly for a "change" event without any further plumbing.
  - PHASE-SPECIFIC DO-NOT-TOUCH respected: no tunable's VALUE was changed anywhere.

VERIFICATION DONE: `python -m py_compile dexter.py` clean. Extracted the exact inserted
source (never imported dexter.py) and exec'd it standalone with stubbed globals — 16

## FEED BADGES + WEEKLY REGRET SPARKLINE (PHASE 7B-4, 2026-07-07, RESTART + DEPLOY)
================================================================================

WHY THIS EXISTS: individual feed calls should age visibly (a skip that would have won
should look different from one that dodged a loser), and the sparkline answers whether
Phases 1-6 actually bent the money-left-on-table curve over calendar time — which the
rest of the counterfactual report, being scoped to BASELINE_TS, structurally can't show.

DISCOVERY:
  (a) Feed render function: `loadFeed()` (fetches `/api/strategy/feed?hours=48&limit=400`)
      populates `_lastFeedData`, then calls `renderFeed()` (builds `.stratFeedCard`
      markup) and `renderRawTable()`. `renderFeed()` was the edit target for badges.
  (b) Charting approach: the page uses TWO different conventions depending on context —
      `renderEquityCurve()` uses a real library (`LightweightCharts.createChart(...)`,
      already loaded), but the funnel bars, reason bars, and heatmap are all hand-rolled
      divs/CSS. A 6-bar weekly sparkline is a glanceable trend strip, not an interactive
      chart, so it was hand-rolled (divs + CSS `height: N%`) matching the funnel/heatmap
      convention — no new library added, per the phase's own instruction.
  (c) `resolved_items` has everything needed for badge matching (symbol, tf, ts, verdict,
      shadow_r) but is baseline-scoped and capped at 300 — confirmed via real data that
      weekly bucketing from it alone would be materially wrong (see THE CHANGE below).

THE CHANGE, PART (a) — feed badges (webapp/index.html only):
  - New CSS: `.stratShadowBadge` (+ `.dodged`/`.missed`/`.pending` color variants) — reuses
    `.stratDecPill`'s pill shape/sizing but with a dashed violet border, the same
    quarantine accent as the rest of the shadow section, so it can never read as a real
    decision pill.
  - New pure JS, added right before `renderFeed()`: `_shadowParseTs(ts)` (normalizes both
    timestamp formats in play — chev_decisions.jsonl's `"YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS"` vs
    resolved_items' `"YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ"`, sourced from labeller's `_now_iso()`), and
    `shadowBadgeForSkip(d, resolvedItems, nowMs)` — matches a feed SKIP record to a
    resolved_items entry by symbol+tf+timestamp within ±5 minutes (closest wins). Returns
    `{kind:'dodged', shadow_r}` (verdict "right"), `{kind:'missed', shadow_r}` (verdict
    "wrong"), `{kind:'unresolved'}` (no match, but the skip is within
    `SHADOW_UNRESOLVED_GRACE_MS` = 48h + the longest EXPIRY_HOURS, swing — a timing fact,
    not a guessed outcome), or `null` (no match, old enough that any outcome could exist —
    silence over guesses, exactly as the phase's own instruction requires). Wired into
    `renderFeed()`'s template for SKIP cards only.
  - `renderFeed()` is re-invoked once more at the end of `loadAll()` (after `loadFeed()`
    and `loadShadow()` — which populates `_shadowResolvedItemsCache` — have both settled),
    mirroring the exact `applyShadowSplitsToReasonBars()` pattern from PHASE 7B-2, since
    `loadFeed`/`loadShadow` run concurrently in the same `Promise.all` and the very first
    paint each cycle could otherwise miss badges depending on which resolves first.
    `renderFeed()` is cheap, idempotent, and driven only off globals — safe to call twice.
  - PURE-HELPER VERIFICATION (paste-run in the browser console, or run via `node` as an
    exact equivalent — both are literally the same JS): fixtures used —
    `resolvedItems = [{symbol:'BTCUSDT',tf:'1h',ts:'2026-07-06T12:03:00Z',verdict:'right',
    shadow_r:-1.2}, {symbol:'ETHUSDT',tf:'15m',ts:'2026-07-06T09:00:00Z',verdict:'wrong',
    shadow_r:0.85}, {symbol:'XRPUSDT',tf:'5m',ts:'2026-07-01T00:00:00Z',verdict:'right',
    shadow_r:-0.4}]`, `NOW = Date.parse('2026-07-10T00:00:00Z')` — 10 cases: exact match
    within 5min → dodged/missed with the right `shadow_r`; match 10min off + old skip →
    null; no match + recent skip → unresolved; no match + old skip → null (not a guessed
    unresolved); same symbol wrong tf → no cross-tf match; null/missing ts → null, no
    throw; exact 5:00-boundary delta → still matches (confirms `<=`, not stricter). All 10
    passed. Confirmed the live inserted function is byte-identical to the tested copy.

THE CHANGE, PART (b) — weekly regret sparkline:
  - counterfactual_report.py: new `_week_start(dt)` (Monday 00:00 UTC of dt's week) and
    `build_weekly_regret(closed_all, weeks=6, now=None)` — computed over the FULL
    `closed_all` list `build_counterfactual()` already loads (no extra file read),
    filtered to SKIP+NOT_ESCALATED with a numeric label and non-None `realized_R` (same
    shadow-trackable universe as everywhere else), bucketed by ISO week, summing
    `forfeited_r` (net>0) / `dodged_r` (net<=0, abs) / `n_resolved` per week. Returns the
    last `weeks` weeks oldest-first, INCLUDING zero-record weeks (an empty week is a real,
    honest data point). Exposed as `build_counterfactual()`'s new `"weekly"` key — the
    ONE field in that dict NOT scoped to `baseline_ts` and NOT subject to
    `RESOLVED_ITEMS_CAP`, clearly flagged as such in the function's own docstring.
    WHY THIS NEEDED A REAL BACKEND CHANGE (not just client-side math): confirmed with
    real data before writing any frontend code — `labels_closed.jsonl`'s records split
    into 2 week-buckets so far, 2026-06-29 (2222 raw records) and 2026-07-06 (1134) — but
    `resolved_items` is deliberately scoped to `BASELINE_TS` (2026-07-06 04:26) onward and
    capped at 300 records, so a client-side-only weekly view would have completely missed
    the entire 2026-06-29 week (1719+ of its resolved SKIP/NOT_ESCALATED records) — exactly
    the history the sparkline exists to show whether Phases 1-6 improved. This is the
    scenario the phase's own escape hatch ("extend the SHARED backend function... never
    compute in two places") was written for.
  - `build_report()` (.txt) gained a matching "WEEKLY REGRET TREND" section, explicitly
    noting it ignores `BASELINE_TS` on purpose, so the .txt and the JSON endpoint still
    never disagree.
  - dexter.py: the `/api/strategy/counterfactual` route's response now includes `"weekly":
    data["weekly"]` alongside the existing public-schema keys.
  - webapp/index.html: new CSS (`.stratSparkRow`/`.stratSparkBar`/`.stratSparkLabels`,
    hand-rolled bars) + markup (`#stratShadowSpark`/`#stratShadowSparkLabels`) inside the
    Shadow Outcomes box, below the Shadow Combo Leaderboard. New JS `renderShadowSparkline
    (weekly)`, called from `loadShadow()` using the SAME already-fetched response (no new
    HTTP request) — bar height ∝ `forfeited_r` (the metric named in the phase spec), a
    2%-minimum floor so zero-weeks still render as a visible sliver rather than vanishing,
    full numbers (forfeited/dodged/n) in each bar's tooltip.
